  <script>
   // Variables and functions for LiveRamp-Tags (former 'Faktor')
    var LR = {
        hasOrganizationConsent: false, // Will be changed by LiveRamp trigger
        scripts: {},
        _allowedScriptNames: [],
        onConsentChanged: [],

        /**
         * 'Register' a callback. It will be fired when you call 'executeAsyncScript' with the same name
         * If 'handleAsyncScript' is called after 'executeAsyncScript', callback from 'handleAsyncScript' with the same name will be fired immediately
         *
         * @param  name
         * @param  cb
         */
        handleAsyncScript: function(name, cb) {
            console.debug('LiveRamp: handleAsyncScript', name);
            if(this._allowedScriptNames.indexOf(name) !== -1) {
                console.debug('LiveRamp: ...execute', name);
                cb();
            } else {
                this.scripts[name] = cb;
            }
        },

        /**
         * Fire a callback, added via 'handleAsyncScript'
         * If 'handleAsyncScript' is called after 'executeAsyncScript', callback from 'handleAsyncScript' with the same name will be fired immediately
         *
         * @param  name
         */
        executeAsyncScript: function(name) {
            console.debug('LiveRamp: executeAsyncScript', name);
            this._allowedScriptNames.push(name); //

            if(this.scripts[name]) {
                console.debug('LiveRamp: ...execute', name);
                this.scripts[name]();
                delete this.scripts[name];
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * Inject and load Javascript from external sources
     *
     * @param  src
     * @param  async
     * @param  location HTMLElement that will be replaced with the injected script tag. If not set, script tag will be added to the head-section as child
     * @param  onLoad
     * @param  onError
     * @param  defer
     */
    function loadScript(src, async, location, onLoad, onError, defer) {
        console.debug('loading script '+src);
        var script = document.createElement('SCRIPT');
        script.onload = onLoad;
        script.onerror = onError;
        script.src = src;

        if(async) {
            script.async = 'async';
        }

        if(defer) {
            script.defer = 'defer';
        }

        if(location) {
            location.parentNode.replaceChild(script, location);
        } else {
            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Fire a callback, when DOM is interactive (either immediately or on event)
     *
     * @param  cb callback function
     */
    function onInteractive(cb) {
        if(document.readyState === 'interactive' || document.readyState === 'complete') {
            console.debug('LiveRamp onInteractive: Call cb immediately');
            cb();
        } else {
            console.debug('LiveRamp onInteractive: Wait for document to be interactive');
            document.addEventListener('readystatechange', function () {
                console.debug('LiveRamp onInteractive: readyState changed to', document.readyState);
                if (document.readyState === 'interactive') {
                    console.debug('LiveRamp onInteractive: ...execute cb');
                    cb();
                }
            });
        }
    }
  </script>
  <script src="https://gdpr-wrapper.privacymanager.io/gdpr/99ede679-2857-4ef9-baa5-c827b4f7502f/gdpr-liveramp.js">
  </script>
  <script>
   // Additional LR functions that need the __tcfapi-Object
    /**
     * Get a collection of purpose and vendor consents.
     * Each consent will be returned as boolean (hasConsent) and string (asString) which might also be 'not-set' if there is no consent yet
     *
     * @param  purposeIds
     * @param  vendorIds
     * @returns  {Promise<unknown>}
     */
    LR.getMixedConsentData = function(purposeIds = null, vendorIds = []) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
            let gotPurposes = false;
            let gotVendors = false;
            let out = {
                purposeConsents: [],
                vendorConsents: []
            };

            __tcfapi('consentDataExist', 2, function(dataExists) {
                console.debug('LiveRamp: consentDataExist', dataExists);
                if(dataExists === true) {
                    sendConsents();
                } else {
                    sendNotSets();
                }
            });

            function sendNotSets() {
                // Purposes
                for(let i=1; i<=30; i++) {
                    out.purposeConsents.push({purposeId: i, hasConsent: false, asString: 'not-set'});
                }

                // Vendors
                vendorIds.forEach((id) => {
                    out.vendorConsents.push({vendorId: id, hasConsent: false, asString: 'not-set'});
                })
            }

            function sendConsents() {
                function checkResolve() {
                    if (gotPurposes && gotVendors) {
                        console.debug('LiveRamp getMixedConsents:',out);
                        resolve(out);
                    }
                }

                __tcfapi('getFullTCData', 2, (tcData) => {
                    const consentData = tcData.purpose.consents;
                    for (let purpose in consentData) {
                        if (purposeIds === null || purposeIds.indexOf(parseInt(purpose)) !== -1) {
                            out.purposeConsents.push({purposeId: parseInt(purpose), hasConsent: consentData[purpose], asString: consentData[purpose].toString()});
                        }
                    }

                    gotPurposes = true;
                    checkResolve();
                });

                let dataObj = vendorIds.map((id) => {
                    return {
                        vendorId: id
                    }
                });

                __tcfapi('checkConsent', 2, (data) => {
                    out.vendorConsents = data.map((v) => {
                        v.asString = v.hasConsent.toString();
                        return v;
                    });

                    gotVendors = true;
                    checkResolve();
                }, {
                    data: dataObj,
                    recheckConsentOnChange: false,
                    perVendor: true
                });
            }
        });
    }

    // Scripts that don't need extra consent handling
    function executeTCFScripts() {
        LR.executeAsyncScript('1plusX');
        LR.executeAsyncScript('smart');
        LR.executeAsyncScript('keywordr');
    }

    __tcfapi('consentDataExist', 2, function(dataExists) {
        console.debug('LiveRamp: consentDataExist', dataExists);
        if(dataExists === true) {
            executeTCFScripts();
        }
    });

    __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function() {
        console.debug('LiveRamp: event consentChanged');
        LR.onConsentChanged.forEach(function(func) {
            if(typeof func === 'function') {
                func();
            }
        });

        // Won't do anything if already called in 'consentDataExist'
        executeTCFScripts();
    }, 'consentChanged');
  </script>

   LR.handleAsyncScript('piano-abd', function() {
            document.cookie = "__adblocker=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT; path=/";
            var setNptTechAdblockerCookie = function(adblocker) {
                var d = new Date();
                d.setTime(d.getTime() + 60 * 5 * 1000);
                document.cookie = "__adblocker=" + (adblocker ? "true" : "false") + "; expires=" + d.toUTCString() + "; path=/";
            };
            var script = document.createElement("script");
            script.setAttribute("async", true);
            script.setAttribute("src", "//www.npttech.com/advertising.js");
            script.setAttribute("onerror", "setNptTechAdblockerCookie(true);");
            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
        });
  </script>

                'gtm.start':
                    new Date().getTime(), event: 'gtm.js'
            });

            j.async = true;
            j.src =
                'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id=' + i + dl;
            f.parentNode.insertBefore(j, f);

            <div class="card__lead">

            <h3 class="card__title">
             <a class="card__link" href="https://www.diepresse.com/5954890/die-drahtzieher-der-corona-demo">

              <span class="hyphenate">
               Gewinnabschöpfung
              </span>
              für mehr Impfdosen in EU?
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="card__lead">
             Ausfuhrzölle nach Maßgabe der Preisunterschiede in der EU und auf dem Weltmarkt könnten helfen, die Versorgung mit Impfstoff zu verbessern. „Impfstoffnationalismus“ müsste sich Europa deshalb nicht vorwerfen lassen.

            <h3 class="card__title">
             <a class="card__link" href="https://www.diepresse.com/5953790/kunst-des-fuhrens-der-weg-zum-offizier">
              Kunst des Führens: Der Weg zum Offizier
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="card__lead">
             <strong>
              Ausbildung.
             </strong>
             An der Theresianischen Militärakademie Wiener Neustadt werden mit dem FH-Bachelorstudiengang „Militärische Führung“ und einem Truppenoffizierslehrgang Offiziere ausgebildet – ab 2022 auch IKT-Offiziere.

            <h3 class="card__title">
             <a class="card__link" href="https://www.diepresse.com/5954907/das-ungluckskleid-gibt-es-wirklich">
              <svg class="premium-badge premium-badge--l" viewbox="0 0 28 28" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
               <title>
                Premium
               </title>
               <path d="M14,0A14,14,0,1,0,28,14,14,14,0,0,0,14,0Zm-.29,7.53a5.87,5.87,0,0,0-1.27.14V19.24c0,1.1.09,1.22.84,1.38l.77.16V21h-6v-.26l.64-.14c.67-.16.76-.22.76-1.4V8.8c0-1.15-.09-1.23-.76-1.39L8.1,7.26V7H14c3.36,0,5,1.26,5,4,0,2.37-1.42,4.24-4.77,4.24a4.68,4.68,0,0,1-1.25-.14v-.35c2.28,0,3-.87,3-3.59S15.36,7.53,13.71,7.53ZM17.88,21a1.32,1.32,0,1,1,1.31-1.31A1.32,1.32,0,0,1,17.88,21Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
              Das
              <span class="hyphenate">
               Unglückskleid
              </span>
              gibt es wirklich
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="card__lead">
             In der Galerie Lisi Hämmerle tritt Schriftstellerin Monika Helfer erstmals auch als bildende Künstlerin in Erscheinung. Ihre Komplizin dabei ist Fotografin Sabine Morgenstern.

            <h3 class="card__title">

            </h3>
            <div class="card__lead">

            <h3 class="card__title">
             <a class="card__link" href="https://www.diepresse.com/5954535/die-grossen-ferien-sind-schon-da">
              Die großen Ferien sind schon da
             </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="card__lead">
             Ein „Update der Romantik“ propagiert die heimische Band Bilderbuch mit ihren ersten neuen Songs seit „Vernissage My Heart“ (2019). „Daydrinking“ heißt der andere.

  <script>
   window.smart_query_prefill = [];

    /** timout after which the api request shall be cancelled */
    let SCRIPT_TIMEOUT = 500,
        WEATHER_INDEX_DEFAULT = -1,
        DEFAULT_DATA_SET = {
            'curr_situation': {situation: -1},
            'curr_temperature': {temp: 273.15}
        },
        handleResponse = (function () {
            /** processed flag to check if script has already been
             processed */
            var processed = false;
            return function (data) {
                /** don't process script twice */
                if (processed) return;
                processed = true;
                /** in case of script loadtime exceeds
                 SCRIPT_TIMEOUT, handleResponse will be called without data. so we'll set a
                 default value here */
                data = data || DEFAULT_DATA_SET;
                /** include weather situation index in whatever
                 kind of ad */

                smart_query_prefill.push("situation=" + data.curr_situation.situation);
                smart_query_prefill.push("temp=" + data.curr_temperature.temp);
            };
        }());
  </script>
  <!-- /Ubimet Weather targeting -->
  <!-- Ubimet API -->
  <script>
   "use strict";
        /** fire ad without weather data after some time */
        window.setTimeout(handleResponse, SCRIPT_TIMEOUT);
  </script>
